Problem 1: 

(VAR vu95NonEmpty x y)
(THEORY 
(AC plus times))
(RULES
num0(S) -> S
minus(x,y) -> plus(opp(y),x)
opp(num0(x)) -> num0(opp(x))
opp(num1(x)) -> j(opp(x))
opp(S) -> S
opp(j(x)) -> num1(opp(x))
plus(num0(x),num0(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
plus(num0(x),num1(y)) -> num1(plus(x,y))
plus(num0(x),j(y)) -> j(plus(x,y))
plus(num1(x),num1(y)) -> j(plus(num1(S),plus(x,y)))
plus(num1(x),j(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
plus(S,x) -> x
plus(j(x),j(y)) -> num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y)))
times(num0(x),y) -> num0(times(x,y))
times(num1(x),y) -> plus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
times(S,x) -> S
times(j(x),y) -> minus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
)


Problem 1: 

Dependency Pairs Processor:
-> FAxioms:
 PLUS(plus(x3,x4),x5) = PLUS(x3,plus(x4,x5))
 PLUS(x3,x4) = PLUS(x4,x3)
 TIMES(times(x3,x4),x5) = TIMES(x3,times(x4,x5))
 TIMES(x3,x4) = TIMES(x4,x3)
-> Pairs:
 MINUS(x,y) -> OPP(y)
 MINUS(x,y) -> PLUS(opp(y),x)
 OPP(num0(x)) -> NUM0(opp(x))
 OPP(num0(x)) -> OPP(x)
 OPP(num1(x)) -> OPP(x)
 OPP(j(x)) -> OPP(x)
 PLUS(num0(x),num0(y)) -> NUM0(plus(x,y))
 PLUS(num0(x),num0(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num0(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num0(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num0(y)),x3) -> NUM0(plus(x,y))

 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num0(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)

 PLUS(plus(num1(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),j(y)),x3) -> NUM0(plus(x,y))
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num0(plus(x,y)),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(S,x),x3) -> PLUS(x,x3)
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y))),x3)
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(j(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num1(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(num1(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(num1(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num1(x),j(y)) -> NUM0(plus(x,y))
 PLUS(num1(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(j(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(j(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(j(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 TIMES(num0(x),y) -> NUM0(times(x,y))
 TIMES(num0(x),y) -> TIMES(x,y)
 TIMES(times(num0(x),y),x3) -> NUM0(times(x,y))
 TIMES(times(num0(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(num0(times(x,y)),x3)
 TIMES(times(num0(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(x,y)
 TIMES(times(num1(x),y),x3) -> NUM0(times(x,y))
 TIMES(times(num1(x),y),x3) -> PLUS(num0(times(x,y)),y)
 TIMES(times(num1(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(plus(num0(times(x,y)),y),x3)
 TIMES(times(num1(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(x,y)
 TIMES(times(S,x),x3) -> TIMES(S,x3)
 TIMES(times(j(x),y),x3) -> NUM0(times(x,y))
 TIMES(times(j(x),y),x3) -> MINUS(num0(times(x,y)),y)
 TIMES(times(j(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(minus(num0(times(x,y)),y),x3)
 TIMES(times(j(x),y),x3) -> TIMES(x,y)
 TIMES(num1(x),y) -> NUM0(times(x,y))
 TIMES(num1(x),y) -> PLUS(num0(times(x,y)),y)
 TIMES(num1(x),y) -> TIMES(x,y)

The problem is decomposed in 3 subproblems.

Problem 1.1: 

Reduction Pairs Processor:
-> FAxioms:
 PLUS(plus(x3,x4),x5) = PLUS(x3,plus(x4,x5))
 PLUS(x3,x4) = PLUS(x4,x3)
-> Pairs:
 PLUS(num0(x),num0(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num0(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num0(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num0(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num0(plus(x,y)),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num0(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num1(plus(x,y)),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(j(plus(x,y)),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num0(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num1(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(j(plus(num1(S),plus(x,y))),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),num1(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num0(plus(x,y)),x3)
 PLUS(plus(num1(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(plus(S,x),x3) -> PLUS(x,x3)
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y))),x3)
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(j(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(plus(j(x),j(y)),x3) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num1(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(num1(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(num1(x),num1(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(num1(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)
 PLUS(j(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(j(S),plus(x,y))
 PLUS(j(x),j(y)) -> PLUS(x,y)

 plus(j(x),j(y)) -> num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y)))
